g ^mH7atMNZ

Conclusion: 
1) 2a + c = pi
2) 2d + f = pi
3) c+f+g = 2pi

Circle Theorem Proof:
1) g = 2pi-c-f
2) 2a+2d+c+f = 2pi
3) g = 2a+2d+c+f -c-f
4) g = 2a+2d
5) g = 2(a+d)
